Unified Alerting Rule Evaluation to Notification Chain\\n\\nThe Grafana unified alerting system implements a complete pipeline for evaluating alert rules and dispatching notifications. This flow is orchestrated through several interconnected components in the `pkg/services/ngalert` package.\\n\\n### Initialization and Service Setup\\nThe entire alerting service is initialized via `ProvideService()` in `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`, which creates the AlertNG struct. This initialization sets up four key components:\\n1. **Rule Scheduler**: Created via `schedule.NewScheduler()` with the state manager\\n2. **State Manager**: Created via `state.NewManager()` to track alert state transitions\\n3. **Alerts Router**: Created via `sender.NewAlertsRouter()` to route alerts to alertmanagers\\n4. **Multi-Org Alertmanager**: Created via `notifier.NewMultiOrgAlertmanager()` to manage per-organization alertmanagers\\n\\n### Rule Scheduling and Evaluation\\nThe rule scheduler in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go` implements the `ScheduleService` interface. The `Run()` method starts the scheduler, which continuously:\\n1. Creates a ticker at the configured base interval\\n2. Calls `schedulePeriodic()` to process ticks\\n3. In each tick, `processTick()` loads alert rules from the store and determines which rules need evaluation\\n4. For each rule requiring evaluation, the scheduler creates or reuses an `alertRule` goroutine from the rule registry\\n\\nEach individual alert rule is executed as a long-lived goroutine implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`. The `alertRule.Run()` method:\\n1. Maintains channels for receiving evaluation requests (`evalCh`) and updates (`updateCh`)\\n2. Processes evaluation requests by calling `evaluate()`\\n3. Manages rule state resets and updates when the rule definition changes\\n\\n### Rule Condition Evaluation\\nDuring evaluation, `alertRule.evaluate()` creates a rule evaluator using the `EvaluatorFactory` from `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`. The factory builds a `ConditionEvaluator` that:\\n1. Constructs an expression pipeline containing datasource queries and expressions\\n2. Calls `Evaluate()` which executes the pipeline via the expression service\\n3. Converts the raw backend response to alert results using `EvaluateAlert()`\\n4. Each result contains alert instance data (labels, annotations, values)\\n\\n### Alert State Transition\\nAfter evaluation, `alertRule.evaluate()` calls `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` from `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`. This critical function:\\n1. Takes the evaluation results and alert rule metadata\\n2. Calls `setNextStateForRule()` to determine state transitions for each alert instance\\n3. Processes missing series states to handle resolved alerts\\n4. Updates the `LastSentAt` field for alerts that need notification\\n5. Persists states to the instance store and state history via the configured persister\\n6. Records state transitions to the historian for state history tracking\\n7. Invokes the `send` callback with `StateTransitions` containing alerts that need to be sent\\n\\nThe `State` struct in `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` tracks:\\n- Current alert state (Normal, Alerting, Resolved, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n- Fired timestamp (when state first transitioned to Alerting)\\n- Resolved timestamp (when state transitioned back to Normal)\\n- Labels and annotations (after template evaluation)\\n- Evaluation results and errors\\n- Image for visualization in notifications\\n\\n### Notification Dispatch\\nThe state transitions flow to the `alertRule.send()` method, which:\\n1. Converts `StateTransition` objects to `PostableAlert` format\\n2. Calls `alertsSender.Send()` which is implemented by `AlertsRouter` in `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`\\n\\nThe `AlertsRouter.Send()` method:\\n1. Retrieves the organization's alert routing configuration (internal vs external alertmanager)\\n2. For internal alertmanager: Routes alerts to `MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts()`\\n3. For external alertmanager: Sends to configured external Alertmanager instances via HTTP\\n4. Maintains separate send queues and managers for external alertmanagers per organization\\n\\n### Internal Alertmanager Processing\\nThe `MultiOrgAlertmanager` in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`:\\n1. Maintains per-organization `alertmanager` instances (Prometheus Alertmanager forks)\\n2. Each organization can have its own alerting configuration\\n3. Wraps `alertingNotify.GrafanaAlertmanager` which is a Prometheus Alertmanager implementation\\n2. Implements alert grouping, silencing, inhibition, and deduplication logic\\n3. Routes alerts to receivers based on notification policies and routing trees\\n4. Manages silences and notification state via `nflog` (notification log) and silences state\\n5. Calls `PutAlerts()` to inject alerts into the processing pipeline\\n\\n### Notification Receiver Integration\\nThe `ReceiverService` in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/receiver_svc.go`:\\n1. Manages notification receivers (email, webhook, Slack, etc.)\\n2. Encrypts/decrypts sensitive receiver data\\n3. Handles receiver creation, update, and deletion\\n4. Validates receiver configurations before applying\\n5. Manages receiver-to-rule associations in notification settings\\n\\n### External Notification Sending\\nFor external alertmanagers, the `ExternalAlertmanager` in `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go`:\\n1. Maintains HTTP connections to remote Alertmanager instances\\n2. Uses a queue-based system to batch and send alerts\\n3. Implements exponential backoff for retries\\n4. Handles service discovery and multi-alertmanager routing\\n5. Sanitizes labels according to UTF-8 support flags\\n\\n### Complete Evaluation Pipeline Summary\\n1. **Scheduler** (schedule.go): Determines when rules need evaluation at configured intervals\\n2. **Rule Executor** (alert_rule.go): Executes individual alert rules with retry logic\\n3. **Evaluator** (eval.go): Executes datasource queries and expressions to evaluate rule conditions\\n4. **State Processor** (manager.go): Determines state transitions and identifies alerts to send\\n5. **Router** (router.go): Routes alerts to internal or external alertmanagers\\n6. **Internal Alertmanager** (alertmanager.go): Processes alerts with grouping, silencing, and deduplication\\n7. **Receivers** (receiver_svc.go): Send notifications via configured channels\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to:\\n- Evaluate complex alert rules with multiple datasources\\n- Maintain alert state across restarts\\n- Support both internal and external alertmanager configurations\\n- Route alerts based on flexible notification policies\\n- Handle high-frequency alert evaluation efficiently\\n- Provide state history and audit trails\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":192,"cache_read_input_tokens":77142,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":192},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ca45df83-7b44-4223-b0ec-4b196ee065f4","uuid":"26d34294-6444-4434-87a6-2b5c41aca572"}

Processes missing series states to handle resolved alerts\\n4. Updates the `LastSentAt` field for alerts that need notification\\n5. Persists states to the instance store and state history via the configured persister\\n6. Records state transitions to the historian for state history tracking\\n7. to Notification Chain\\n\\nThe Grafana unified alerting system implements a complete pipeline for evaluating alert rules and dispatching notifications. This flow is orchestrated through several interconnected components in the `pkg/services/ngalert` package.\\n\\n### Initialization and Service Setup\\nThe entire alerting service is initialized via `ProvideService()` in `pkg/services/ngalert/ngalert.go`, which creates the AlertNG struct. This initialization sets up four key components:\\n1. **Rule Scheduler**: Created via `schedule.NewScheduler()` with the state manager\\n2. **State Manager**: Created via `state.NewManager()` to track alert state transitions\\n3. **Alerts Router**: Created via `sender.NewAlertsRouter()` to route alerts to alertmanagers\\n4. **Multi-Org Alertmanager**: Created via `notifier.NewMultiOrgAlertmanager()` to manage per-organization alertmanagers\\n\\n### Rule Scheduling and Evaluation\\nThe rule scheduler in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go` implements the `ScheduleService` interface. The `Run()` method starts the scheduler, which continuously:\\n1. Creates a ticker at the configured base interval\\n2. Calls `schedulePeriodic()` to process ticks\\n3. In each tick, `processTick()` loads alert rules from the store and determines which rules need evaluation\\n4. For each rule requiring evaluation, the scheduler creates or reuses an `alertRule` goroutine from the rule registry\\n\\nEach individual alert rule is executed as a long-lived goroutine implemented in `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`. The `alertRule.Run()` method:\\n1. Maintains channels for receiving evaluation requests (`evalCh`) and updates (`updateCh`)\\n2. Processes evaluation requests by calling `evaluate()`\\n3. Manages rule state resets and updates when the rule definition changes\\n\\n### Rule Condition Evaluation\\nDuring evaluation, `alertRule.evaluate()` creates a rule evaluator using the `EvaluatorFactory` from `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`. The factory builds a `ConditionEvaluator` that:\\n1. Constructs an expression pipeline containing datasource queries and expressions\\n2. Calls `Evaluate()` which executes the pipeline via the expression service\\n3. Converts the raw backend response to alert results using `EvaluateAlert()`\\n4. Each result contains alert instance data (labels, annotations, values)\\n\\n### Alert State Transition\\nAfter evaluation, `alertRule.evaluate()` calls `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` from `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`. This critical function:\\n1. Takes the evaluation results and alert rule metadata\\n2. Calls `setNextStateForRule()` to determine state transitions for each alert instance\\n3. Processes missing series states to handle resolved alerts\\n4. Updates the `LastSentAt` field for alerts that need notification\\n5. Persists states to the instance store and state history via the configured persister\\n6. Records state transitions to the historian for state history tracking\\n7. Invokes the `send` callback with `StateTransitions` containing alerts that need to be sent\\n\\nThe `State` struct in `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` tracks:\\n- Current alert state (Normal, Alerting, Resolved, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n- Fired timestamp (when state first transitioned to Alerting)\\n- Resolved timestamp (when state transitioned back to Normal)\\n- Labels and annotations (after template evaluation)\\n- Evaluation results and errors\\n- Image for visualization in notifications\\n\\n### Notification Dispatch\\nThe state transitions flow to the `alertRule.send()` method, which:\\n1. Converts `StateTransition` objects to `PostableAlert` format\\n2. Calls `alertsSender.Send()` which is implemented by `AlertsRouter` in `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`\\n\\nThe `AlertsRouter.Send()` method:\\n1. Retrieves the organization's alert routing configuration (internal vs external alertmanager)\\n2. For internal alertmanager: Routes alerts to `MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts()`\\n3. For external alertmanager: Sends to configured external Alertmanager instances via HTTP\\n4. Maintains separate send queues and managers for external alertmanagers per organization\\n\\n### Internal Alertmanager Processing\\nThe `MultiOrgAlertmanager` in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`:\\n1. Maintains per-organization `alertmanager` instances (Prometheus Alertmanager forks)\\n2. Each organization can have its own alerting configuration\\n3. When alerts arrive via `PutAlerts()`, they are forwarded to the org's alertmanager instance\\n\\nThe internal `alertmanager` in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/alertmanager.go`:\\n1. Wraps `alertingNotify.GrafanaAlertmanager` which is a Prometheus Alertmanager implementation\\n2. Implements alert grouping, silencing, inhibition, and deduplication logic\\n3. Routes alerts to receivers based on notification policies and routing trees\\n4. Manages silences and notification state via `nflog` (notification log) and silences state\\n5. Calls `PutAlerts()` to inject alerts into the processing pipeline\\n\\n### Notification Receiver Integration\\nThe `ReceiverService` in `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/receiver_svc.go`:\\n1. Manages notification receivers (email, webhook, Slack, etc.)\\n2. Encrypts/decrypts sensitive receiver data\\n3. Handles receiver creation, update, and deletion\\n4. Validates receiver configurations before applying\\n5. Manages receiver-to-rule associations in notification settings\\n\\n### External Notification Sending\\nFor external alertmanagers, the `ExternalAlertmanager` in `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go`:\\n1. Maintains HTTP connections to remote Alertmanager instances\\n2. Uses a queue-based system to batch and send alerts\\n3. Implements exponential backoff for retries\\n4. Handles service discovery and multi-alertmanager routing\\n5. Sanitizes labels according to UTF-8 support flags\\n\\n### Complete Evaluation Pipeline Summary\\n1. **Scheduler** (schedule.go): Determines when rules need evaluation at configured intervals\\n2. **Rule Executor** (alert_rule.go): Executes individual alert rules with retry logic\\n3. **Evaluator** (eval.go): Executes datasource queries and expressions to evaluate rule conditions\\n4. **State Processor** (manager.go): Determines state transitions and identifies alerts to send\\n5. **Router** (router.go): Routes alerts to internal or external alertmanagers\\n6. **Internal Alertmanager** (alertmanager.go): Processes alerts with grouping, silencing, and deduplication\\n7. **Receivers** (receiver_svc.go): Send notifications via configured channels\\n\\nThis architecture enables Grafana to:\\n- Evaluate complex alert rules with multiple datasources\\n- Maintain alert state across restarts\\n- Support both internal and external alertmanager configurations\\n- Route alerts based on flexible notification policies\\n- Handle high-frequency alert evaluation efficiently\\n- Provide state history and audit trails\"\n    54→}\n    55→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
